event = {
	id = 26001
	random = yes
	country = ADE
	trigger = {
		NOT = { flag = castillian }
	}
	name = "EVENTNAME60"
	desc = "EVENTHIST60"
	action_a = {
		name = "EVENT60A6"
		command = { type = add_countryculture which = iberian }
		command = { type = domestic which = CENTRALIZATION value = -1 }
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
		command = { type = setflag which = castillian }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVENT60B"
		command = { type = stability value = 5 }
		command = { type = badboy value = -5 }
		command = { type = inflation value = -5 }
		command = { type = cash value = 500 }
	}
}

	random = yes
	country = MTR
	trigger = {
		NOT = { flag = upper }
	}
	name = "EVENTNAME60"
	desc = "EVENTHIST60"
	action_a = {
		name = "EVENT60A30"
		command = { type = add_countryculture which = abenaki }
		command = { type = domestic which = CENTRALIZATION value = -1 }
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
		command = { type = setflag which = upper }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVENT60B"
		command = { type = stability value = 5 }
		command = { type = badboy value = -5 }
		command = { type = inflation value = -5 }
		command = { type = cash value = 500 }
	}
}
